In[3]:
import sys
sys.path.append("..")

import json, os
from render_logprobs import render_logprobs

filedir = 'examples_data'

def load_render_logprobs(filename, dir):
    filename = filename + ".json" if not filename.endswith(".json") else filename
    load_path = os.path.join(dir, filename)

    with open(load_path, 'r') as f:
        examples = json.load(f)

    for ex in examples:
        render_logprobs(ex['logprobs'], ex['question'])

Alice, Bob, and Claire are playing a game. At the start of the game, they are each holding a ball: Alice has a pink ball, Bob has a green ball, and Claire has a white ball. As the game progresses, pairs of players trade balls. First, Claire and Alice swap balls. Then, Alice and Bob swap balls. Finally, Bob and Claire swap balls. At the end of the game, Claire has the A) pink ball. B) green ball. C) white ball. (Answer: C)
